   googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
    googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
    googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
    // Collapse wrappers for collapsed slot divs.
    var collapseWrappers = function () {
      var slotIds = Object.keys(googletag.slots)
        .map(function (v) { return '#' + v; });
      jQuery(slotIds.join(','))
        .filter('*[style="display: none;"]')
        .parents('.dfp-tag-wrapper')
        .hide();
    };

    var collapseWrappersDebounce = null;
    googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
      if (event.isEmpty) {
        jQuery('#' + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents('.dfp-tag-wrapper').hide();
      }

      clearTimeout(collapseWrappersDebounce);
      collapseWrappersDebounce = setTimeout(collapseWrappers, 200);
    });

    googletag.enableServices();
  });
